<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:opwinden.html>opwinden</a> (12444)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:opwinden.html>opwinden</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">up</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:winden.html>winden</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wind</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opwinden.html>opwinden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To wind, to wind up; e.g. to tighten a clockwork mechanism</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To agitate, to excite</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To get agitated, to get excited, to become aggravated</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">arance</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">orange</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">orenge</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">arange</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">arancia</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Spanish" class="extiw" title="w:Old Spanish">Old Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osp">naranja</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">نَارَنْج</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nāranj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">نارنگ</i> | , from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">नारङ्ग</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nāraṅga</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dravidian_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Dravidian languages">Dravidian</a></span>.
</p><p>The spelling <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> subsequently influenced by <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">orange</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oranje.html>oranje</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oranje.html>oranjer</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oranje.html>oranje</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">oranjest</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>orange
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sinaasappel.html>sinaasappel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:oranje.html>oranje</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The orange <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>orange</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***orca.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:orca.html>orca</a> (89675)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:orca.html>orca</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tun, cask; whale</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, see there for more. Although the origin <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> obscure, the sometimes-cited association with <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">orcus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">underworld</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> folk-etymology.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:orca.html>orca</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">orcas</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:orca.html>orca</a></strong></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A sea mammal (<i>Orcinus <a href = vnd.unilang:orca.html>orca</a></i>) related to <a href = vnd.unilang:dolphins.html>dolphins</a> and porpoises, commonly called the killer whale.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">grampus</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">killer whale</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">blackfish</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
</body>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Translingualism" class="extiw" title="w:Translingualism">translingual</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="mul">Orchideae</i>, coined by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Linnaeus" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Linnaeus">Linnaeus</a> based on <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">orchis</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ὄρχις</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">órkhis</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***orde.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:orde.html>orde</a> (1361)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ordenen.html>ordene</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:ordenen.html>ordene</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ordō, ordinem</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">organe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">organum</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ὄργανον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">órganon</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">organisation</i>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:organist.html>organist</a> (43261)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:organist.html>organist</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">organista</i>.

</p>
<ol><li>organ player, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:organist.html>organist</a></span>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">orgele</i>, from earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">orgene</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">organa</i>, plural of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">organum</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ὄργανον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">órganon</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:orgel.html>orgel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:orgels.html>orgels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:orgeltje.html>orgeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> organ</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:orgel.html>orgel</a></strong>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:orkaan.html>orkaan</a> (5568)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">huracán</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ta%C3%ADno_language" class="extiw" title="w:Taíno language">Taíno</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tnq">juracán</i>; cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">ouragan</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hurricane</i> (originally <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hurricano</i>); <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Orkan</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> borrowed from Dutch.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:orkaan.html>orkaan</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:orkanen.html>orkanen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:orkaan.html>orkaantje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>hurricane</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An uncontrollable/destructive force</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Something moving extremely fast</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:orkaan.html>orkaan</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:meteorologie.html>meteorologie</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bijzonder.html>bijzonder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hevige.html>hevige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:storm.html>storm</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i>In <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boek.html>boek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stond.html>stond</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ontstaan.html>ontstaan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:orkaan.html>orkaan</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitgelegd.html>uitgelegd</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

***orkest.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:orkest.html>orkest</a> (8953)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">orchestre</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">orchēstra</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ὀρχήστρα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">orkhḗstra</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ὀρχοῦμαι</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">orkhoûmai</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to dance</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (an intensification of <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἔρχομαι</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">érkhomai</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to go, come</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ergh-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to set in motion, stir up, raise</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>) + <a href = vnd.unilang:suffix.html>suffix</a> *<i>-tra</i> denoting "place".
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:orkest.html>orkest</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:orkesten.html>orkesten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:orkestje.html>orkestje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">orchestra</span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:orkest.html>orkest</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:muziek.html>muziek</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:groep.html>groep</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:musici.html>musici</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:orkest.html>orkest</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:staat.html>staat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zacht.html>zacht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:spelen.html>spelen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:erg.html>erg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sterk.html>sterk</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:orsini.html>orsini</a> (35756)</h1><br></body> 
***ort.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ort.html>ort</a> (68219)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:ort.html>ort</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">*orǣt</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">that which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> left after eating</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">out-eat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">or-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">eat</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">orte</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">refuse of food</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ooraete</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ooreete</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:ort.html>ort</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:ort.html>ort</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">urez</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">uräß</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ort.html>ort</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">orts</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">usually in the plural</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A fragment; a scrap of leftover food; any remainder; a piece of refuse.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1861</b>,  George Eliot,  chapter III, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:silas.html>Silas</a> Marner</cite>, page 40:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>the rich <a href = vnd.unilang:eten.html>ate</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:drank.html>drank</a> freely, <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="and accepted gout and apoplexy as things that ran mysteriously in respectable families, and the poor thought that the rich were entirely in the right of it to lead a jolly life; besides,">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> their feasting caused a multiplication of <b>orts</b>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> the heirlooms of the poor.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1922</b>,  James Joyce,  <cite>Ulysses</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Come, Kinch, you have eaten all <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> left. <a href = vnd.unilang:ay.html>Ay</a>, I will serve you your <b>orts</b> and offals.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1997</b>,  Thomas Pynchon,  <cite>Mason amp; Dixon</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Peace, Grandam,– reclaim thy <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ort.html>Ort</a></b>. The Learnèd One <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> yet to sink quite that low.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">fragment</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">bit</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">chip</span>; See also Thesaurus:piece</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">leftover food</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">gubbins</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">leftover</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">scrap</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">any remainder</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">remnant</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">residue</span>; See also Thesaurus:remainder</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">a piece of refuse</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">garbage</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">rubbish</span>; See also Thesaurus:trash</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ort.html>ort</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">orts</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">orting</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">orted</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To turn away from with disgust; refuse.</li></ol>
</body>
